***сиживать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сиживать.html>си́живать</a> (28213)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сидеть.html>сиде́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sidétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сиживать.html>си́живать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">síživatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to sit <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">repeatedly or frequently</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>; <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/iterative_aspect" class="extiw" title="w:iterative aspect">iterative</a> of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сидеть.html>сиде́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sidétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>This is an iterative verb, and in standard language is conjugated only in the infinitive and the past tense.</li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:си.html>си́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>жи<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>вать</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:сидеть.html>сиде́ть</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-сиж-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ива</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сизый.html>си́зый</a> (5896)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">шизый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šizyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Possibly cognate to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сивый.html>си́вый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sívyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>dove-coloured, warm grey, bluish
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сизый.html>си́зый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:голубь.html>го́лубь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sízyj</b> gólubʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">rock dove <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">IOC preferred term</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, rock pigeon</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сизый.html>си́зый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:туман.html>тума́н</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sízyj</b> tumán</i> ― <span class="e-translation">blue-grey mist</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***сила.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́ла</a> (157)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sila</i>. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">síela</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́ла</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">síla</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́лы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́лы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́л</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>strength

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изо.html>и́зо</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всех</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́л</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ízo vsex sil</i> ― <span class="e-translation">with all one's might</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́лах</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne v sílax</i> ― <span class="e-translation">unable</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́лам</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne po sílam</i> ― <span class="e-translation">beyond one’s strength</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свои́ми</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́лами</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">svoími sílami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">by oneself</span></div></dd>

<li>force</li>

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́ла</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">síla</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">strength</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ач</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ač</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***сильный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сильный.html>си́льный</a> (427)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*silьnъ</i>. Synchronically analysable as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́ла</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">síla</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сильный.html>си́льный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sílʹnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)сильне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)сильне́й</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сильнейший.html>сильне́йший</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>strong, powerful
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1886</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anton_Chekhov" class="extiw" title="w:Anton Chekhov">Anton Chekhov</a>,  “The Chorus Girl”, in <span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Please provide the book title or journal name)</span>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:барыня.html>бары́ня</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:встать.html>вста́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сильный.html>си́льном</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:волнение.html>волне́нии</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пройтись.html>прошла́сь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:комната.html>ко́мнате</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Barýnja vstála i v <b>sílʹnom</b> volnénii prošlásʹ po kómnate.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The lady got up and walked about the room in <b>great</b> excitement.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">grammar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> irregular</li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>си́ль<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1*a/c'. 
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>Встреча́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> <span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="устаревшее">устар.</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ударение.html>ударе́ния</a> кр.ф.: <i><a href = vnd.unilang:сильный.html>си́лен</a></i>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-силь-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:порядочный.html>-н</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:симбиоз.html>симбио́з</a> (29366)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:симбиоз.html>симбио́з</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">simbióz</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:симбиоз.html>симбио́за</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:симбиоз.html>симбио́зы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:симбиоз.html>симбио́зов</a></b>)

<ol><li>symbiosis <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">relationship of mutual benefit</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:символ.html>си́мвол</a> (3496)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">σύμβολον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">súmbolon</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Occurrence of <span class="IPA">/v/</span> indicates a relatively late borrowing.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:символ.html>си́мвол</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">símvol</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:символ.html>си́мвола</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:символ.html>си́мволы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:символ.html>си́мволов</a></b>)
</p>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:симпатизировавший.html>симпатизи́ровавший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">simpatizírovavšij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past active imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:симпатизировать.html>симпатизи́ровать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">simpatizírovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сей.html>сим</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:па.html>па</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ти́ч<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-симпат-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ичн</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***симпатия.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:симпатия.html>симпа́тия</a> (5284)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Sympathie</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">sympatia</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:симпатия.html>симпа́тия</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">simpátija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:симпатия.html>симпа́тии</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:симпатия.html>симпа́тии</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:симпатия.html>симпа́тий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>favour; attraction; sympathy
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чувствовать.html>чу́вствовать</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:симпатия.html>симпа́тию</a></b> (<a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> кому́-либо)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">čúvstvovatʹ <b>simpátiju</b> (k komú-libo)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to feel warmly toward someone</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:питать.html>пита́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:симпатия.html>симпа́тию</a></b> (<a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> кому́-либо)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pitátʹ <b>simpátiju</b> (k komú-libo)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to favour someone</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:влечение.html>влече́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vlečénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расположение.html>расположе́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">raspoložénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:антипатия.html>антипа́тия</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">antipátija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sweetheart; darling; flame (<i>a person who is liked or desired</i>)
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">зазно́ба</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zaznóba</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пассия.html>па́ссия</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pássija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:увлечение.html>увлече́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">uvlečénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Although <b>cимпатия</b> is cognate with <b>sympathy</b>, these words may have different connotations. The Russian <b><a href = vnd.unilang:симпатия.html>симпа́тия</a></b> implies attraction, liking or warm feeling, but usually not compassion or condolence.
</p>

***симулировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:симулировать.html>симули́ровать</a> (26938)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">simulieren</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">simulō</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">-ieren</i>, with the Russian suffix <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Morphologically симул- + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ровать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-írovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:симулировать.html>симули́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">simulírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to simulate</li>
<li>to feign an illness or disability, especially in clinical or legal context; to malinger</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">симуля́ция</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">simuljácija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:си.html>си</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ва́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>тый</b>
